        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer552614579" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4046417616980999666">I read this book because it seemed highly recommended, but I don't understand the hype. The author has some good concepts in the book, but that is intertwined in a standard format fantasy adventure. The characters are not very well developed and motivations are questionable. I read the entire book and it was entertaining, but there wasn't that much there. Part of my gripe may be it is meant for a younger audience, but there are still very good books - the Ranger's Apprentice series is a great on</span>
  <span id="freeText4046417616980999666" style="display:none">I read this book because it seemed highly recommended, but I don't understand the hype. The author has some good concepts in the book, but that is intertwined in a standard format fantasy adventure. The characters are not very well developed and motivations are questionable. I read the entire book and it was entertaining, but there wasn't that much there. Part of my gripe may be it is meant for a younger audience, but there are still very good books - the Ranger's Apprentice series is a great one that both talks of a young boy growing up and takes on a series of adult problems. If you want a new author, the Green Rider series is also good. The Fantasy genre seems to have a difficult time differentiating between various books made for different ages. I have read plenty of "YA" books, but this one doesn't do it for me. If you want old school fantasy look into the Dragonlance books by Weiss and Hickman. This author has good concepts, but there is so much else out there that has a more developed story.</span>
  <a data-text-id="4046417616980999666" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <span id="freeText7386580750097737460" style="display:none">Borrowed this from Rhett my brother on CD. This book was not too deep just a LOT of fun.   <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/57853182" />
    <a title="Cynthia" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/358463-cynthia"><img alt="Cynthia" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1189194452p2/358463.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/57853182?book_show_action=true">May 30, 2009</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Cynthia" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Cynthia" href="/user/show/358463-cynthia">Cynthia</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/358463-cynthia?shelf=great-reads">great-reads</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer57853182" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9720098213267058425">I have mixed feelings about this book. Overall I really liked it, but it echoes the plot lines of some familiar favorites. I felt like this book was a mixture of Harry Potter and Lord of the Rings. I never really felt a strong connection with the main character because we don't learn much about him until the end of the book. I also had a hard time keeping his fellow adventurers straight since they're introduced in such rapid succession and the author doesn't take the time to really introduce eac</span>
  <span id="freeText9720098213267058425" style="display:none">I have mixed feelings about this book. Overall I really liked it, but it echoes the plot lines of some familiar favorites. I felt like this book was a mixture of Harry Potter and Lord of the Rings. I never really felt a strong connection with the main character because we don't learn much about him until the end of the book. I also had a hard time keeping his fellow adventurers straight since they're introduced in such rapid succession and the author doesn't take the time to really introduce each one. The title is also a little misleading because the recovery of Slathbog's Gold is a very small part of the book. That said I did think that it was a fun read, full of adventure and suspense and I liked the surprise ending.</span>
  <a data-text-id="9720098213267058425" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer7341353383618863214">My brother recommended this book to me so I thought I'd give it a try. Slathbog's Gold has adventure, action, mystery, magic, everything. It is a great story about a boy who becomes an adventurer and goes on a quest to slay a dragon without knowing anything about adventures and the new world he's found. He learns a lot about this new world on his adventure and makes many new friends. If you love stories about slaying dragons and dwarfs and wizards and elves then I know you are going to love this</span>
  <span id="freeText7341353383618863214" style="display:none">My brother recommended this book to me so I thought I'd give it a try. Slathbog's Gold has adventure, action, mystery, magic, everything. It is a great story about a boy who becomes an adventurer and goes on a quest to slay a dragon without knowing anything about adventures and the new world he's found. He learns a lot about this new world on his adventure and makes many new friends. If you love stories about slaying dragons and dwarfs and wizards and elves then I know you are going to love this book just as much as I did. It's a great story that keeps you hooked with bandits, mysterious oracles, strange dwarves and dangerous dragons. If you want a fast, fun read I would recommend reading this book. </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer3816286827513744482">This is the perfect book for those little readers who can read at a higher level, but may not be mature enough yet for the content of books such as the later Harry Potter books. This is a great fantansy journey, but keeps everything very basic and straight forward, so it's not too scary for those young readers. Older readers may find it a little too basic, and perhaps predictable, but will still appreciate the imagination, and the fun ride. It would be a great read aloud to young kids. All the a</span>
  <span id="freeText3816286827513744482" style="display:none">This is the perfect book for those little readers who can read at a higher level, but may not be mature enough yet for the content of books such as the later Harry Potter books. This is a great fantansy journey, but keeps everything very basic and straight forward, so it's not too scary for those young readers. Older readers may find it a little too basic, and perhaps predictable, but will still appreciate the imagination, and the fun ride. It would be a great read aloud to young kids. All the adventure without anything too scary. Good swashbuckling without descriptive gore. I can imagine many young ones wishing to find an "Adventurers Wanted" sign in their own neighborhood.</span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('2PQe07YIVJSjKQSwJlzbXX6557aS2xXBX1gomzZTmxFHNVdBh3XntJMX3G2lmHpXfVXaKzQQyRxKL/TEceeiTw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('C0mOz5AXkwkA83xTXUuPPmOtIkGtDk90E/KDa/WsOSyUiMddoWogKTDNpI7ejy40YEEf3AvFk6kGhV80shgAcg==')})
  }

<span id="freeTextContainer1780988521068769872">Mark Forman was born and raised in Utah and now resides in the foothills of the western Rockies. He tries to write as much as possible when he's not working as a systems administrator and attending to his many other hobbies, such as fishing, camping, hiking and almost anything that will allow him to enjoy the magic of nature. </span>
